    <script>
    (function () {
      var URL = "https:\/\/fastestlap.com\/wp-json\/grandpx\/v1\/cards?paged=1";
      console.log('[HEAD] fetching GPX cards:', URL);

      var htmlReady = false, htmlText = '', injected = false;

      // Fetch immediately
      console.time('HEAD_GET_cards');
      fetch(URL, { credentials: 'same-origin' })
        .then(function (r) {
          // We expect text/html (raw fragment)
          var hdr = (r.headers && r.headers.get) ? r.headers.get('X-GrandPX-Route') : null;
          if (hdr) console.log('[HEAD] X-GrandPX-Route:', hdr);
          return r.ok ? r.text() : '';
        })
        .then(function (html) {
          console.timeEnd('HEAD_GET_cards');
          htmlText = html || '';
          htmlReady = true;
          tryInject();
        })
        .catch(function (e) {
          console.warn('[HEAD] fetch error:', e);
        });

      function gridEl() { return document.querySelector('.rss-articles-grid'); }

      function tryInject() {
        if (injected || !htmlReady) return;
        var grid = gridEl();
        if (!grid) return; // wait until the grid exists

        if (htmlText) {
          grid.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', htmlText);
          injected = true;
          window.__GPX_FIRST_BATCH_INJECTED = true;

          // Hydrate "VIEWED" state to match plugin behavior
          try {
            var viewed = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('viewedArticles') || '[]');
            grid.querySelectorAll('.rss-article-box').forEach(function (el) {
              var id = +el.getAttribute('data-post-id');
              if (viewed.indexOf(id) !== -1) {
                el.classList.add('article-read');
                if (!el.querySelector('.viewed-label')) {
                  var lab = document.createElement('div');
                  lab.className = 'viewed-label';
                  lab.textContent = 'VIEWED';
                  el.appendChild(lab);
                }
              }
            });
          } catch (e) {}
        }
      }

      // Try once DOM is ready, and also watch for the grid to appear
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', tryInject);
      try {
        new MutationObserver(tryInject).observe(document.documentElement, { childList: true, subtree: true });
      } catch (e) {}
    })();
    </script>

// === Medal progress check === //
function trackMedalIncrement(medalType) {
    gtag('event', 'medal_earned', {
        'event_category': 'medal_progress',
        'event_label': medalType,
        'value': 1
    });
}

function checkMedalCounts() {
    const casualCount = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('casualFanCount')) || 0;
    const avidCount = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('avidFanCount')) || 0;
    const hardcoreCount = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('hardcoreFanCount')) || 0;

    const lastCasualCount = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('lastTrackedCasualCount')) || 0;
    const lastAvidCount = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('lastTrackedAvidCount')) || 0;
    const lastHardcoreCount = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('lastTrackedHardcoreCount')) || 0;

    if (casualCount > lastCasualCount) trackMedalIncrement('Casual');
    if (avidCount > lastAvidCount) trackMedalIncrement('Avid');
    if (hardcoreCount > lastHardcoreCount) trackMedalIncrement('Hardcore');

    localStorage.setItem('lastTrackedCasualCount', casualCount);
    localStorage.setItem('lastTrackedAvidCount', avidCount);
    localStorage.setItem('lastTrackedHardcoreCount', hardcoreCount);
}

// === Dynamic element tracking for articles === //
document.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
    const articleBox = event.target.closest('.rss-article-box');
    if (articleBox) {
        const publisherSpan = articleBox.querySelector('.publisher-time-wrapper span');
        const publisherName = publisherSpan ? publisherSpan.textContent.trim() : 'Unknown Publisher';

        console.log(`Tracking article click for publisher: ${publisherName}`);
        gtag('event', 'article_click', {
            'event_category': 'publisher_tracking',
            'event_label': publisherName,
            'value': 1
        });
    }
});
	
	
document.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
    const progressBar = event.target.closest('#progress-bar, #progress-bar-desktop');
    if (progressBar) {
        console.log('Tracking: checking_stats event fired');
        gtag('event', 'checking_stats', {
            'event_category': 'user_action',
            'event_label': 'Checking Stats',
            'value': 1
        });
    }
});
	
// Track "See the latest news" button
document.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
    const latestNewsBtn = event.target.closest('.flp-latest-btn');
    if (latestNewsBtn) {
        gtag('event', 'latest_news_button', {
            'event_category': 'navigation',
            'event_label': 'Back to homepage from post page',
            'value': 1
        });
        console.log('Latest News button clicked');
    }
});

<!-- HFCM by 99 Robots - Snippet # 7031: Swiper JS header code (reload trap script) -->
<!-- Swiper CSS -->
<link data-minify="1" rel="stylesheet" href="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/cache/min/1/swiper/swiper-bundle.min.css?ver=1770930769" />

<!-- Swiper JS -->
<script src="https://unpkg.com/swiper/swiper-bundle.min.js"></script>


<script>
window.location.reload = function() {
  console.warn("Reload intercepted—stack:", new Error().stack);
};
	
	
	
;(function(){
  // No script on the page can now force a reload:
  const noop = function(...args){
    console.warn('Blocked programmatic navigation:', this, args, new Error().stack);
  };

  // Block reload()
  const origReload = window.location.reload;
  window.location.reload = noop;

  // Block assign() and replace()
  const origAssign  = window.location.assign;
  const origReplace = window.location.replace;
  window.location.assign  = noop;
  window.location.replace = noop;

  // For extra coverage, block calls to setting location.href
  try {
    const proto = Object.getPrototypeOf(window.location);
    ['href','protocol','host','hostname','port','pathname','search','hash']
      .forEach(prop => {
        const desc = Object.getOwnPropertyDescriptor(proto, prop);
        if (desc && desc.set) {
          Object.defineProperty(proto, prop, {
            ...desc,
            set(value) {
              console.warn(`Blocked setting location.${prop} =`, value, new Error().stack);
            }
          });
        }
      });
  } catch(e){
    console.warn("Unable to lock down location setters:", e);
  }
})();
	

</script>
<!-- /end HFCM by 99 Robots -->
<!-- HFCM by 99 Robots - Snippet # 7032: Swiper Popup Initializer -->
<script>
// Declare swiperInitialized to track if Swiper has already been initialized
let swiperInitialized = false;

// Trigger the popup when a medal image is clicked
document.querySelectorAll('#bronze-medal, #silver-medal, #gold-medal').forEach(function(medal) {
    medal.addEventListener('click', function() {
        document.getElementById('badge-popup').style.display = 'block';  // Show the popup

        // Initialize Swiper when the popup is shown
        if (!swiperInitialized) {
            const swiper = new Swiper('#card-flip-container', {
                effect: 'flip',  // Flip effect
                allowTouchMove: true,  // Enable swipe gestures
                flipEffect: {
                    slideShadows: false,  // Disable shadow effect if desired
                },
                loop: false  // No looping since there are only two sides
            });
            swiperInitialized = true;  // Prevent multiple Swiper initializations
        }
    });
});

// Close button functionality
document.getElementById('close-popup').addEventListener('click', function() {
    document.getElementById('badge-popup').style.display = 'none';  // Hide the popup
});

</script>

<!-- HFCM by 99 Robots - Snippet # 7037: Tracking Events &amp; scripts -->
<script>
// Track when the user starts the game
document.getElementById('game-toggle-button').addEventListener('click', function() {
    gtag('event', 'game_start', {
        'event_category': 'game_interaction',
        'event_label': 'Reaction Time Game Start',
        'value': 1
    });
});

// Track when the user shares their score
document.getElementById('share-button').addEventListener('click', function() {
    gtag('event', 'score_share', {
        'event_category': 'game_interaction',
        'event_label': 'Score Shared',
        'value': 1
    });
});

// Track in-app refresh button
document.getElementById('notification-popup').addEventListener('click', function() {
    gtag('event', 'inapp_update', {
        'event_category': 'user_action',
        'event_label': 'In-app Update Button Clicked',
        'value': 1
    });
});

// Track test-my-speed button
document.getElementById('start-button').addEventListener('click', function() {
    gtag('event', 'test_my_speed', {
        'event_category': 'game_interaction',
        'event_label': 'Test My Speed Button Clicked',
        'value': 1
    });
});

//Track Retry button
document.getElementById('retry-button').addEventListener('click', function() {
    gtag('event', 'retry_game', {
        'event_category': 'game_interaction',
        'event_label': 'Retry Button Clicked',
        'value': 1
    });
});

// Select all medal elements by their IDs (adjust these IDs if necessary)
const medals = document.querySelectorAll('#bronze-medal, #silver-medal, #gold-medal');

// Loop through each medal and add a click event listener
medals.forEach(medal => {
    medal.addEventListener('click', function() {
        // Send a custom event to Google Analytics when a medal is clicked
        gtag('event', 'game_card_open', {
            'event_category': 'popup_interaction',
            'event_label': 'Badge Popup Viewed',
            'value': 1
        });
    });
});

	// Function to track a medal increment in Google Analytics
function trackMedalIncrement(medalType) {
    gtag('event', 'medal_earned', {
        'event_category': 'medal_progress',
        'event_label': medalType, // This could be 'Casual', 'Avid', or 'Hardcore'
        'value': 1
    });
}

// Function to check for updates in medal counts
function checkMedalCounts() {
    // Retrieve current counts from localStorage
    const casualCount = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('casualFanCount')) || 0;
    const avidCount = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('avidFanCount')) || 0;
    const hardcoreCount = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('hardcoreFanCount')) || 0;

    // Retrieve previously tracked counts from localStorage (or initialize)
    const lastCasualCount = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('lastTrackedCasualCount')) || 0;
    const lastAvidCount = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('lastTrackedAvidCount')) || 0;
    const lastHardcoreCount = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('lastTrackedHardcoreCount')) || 0;

    // Check for increments and track accordingly
    if (casualCount > lastCasualCount) {
        trackMedalIncrement('Casual');
    }
    if (avidCount > lastAvidCount) {
        trackMedalIncrement('Avid');
    }
    if (hardcoreCount > lastHardcoreCount) {
        trackMedalIncrement('Hardcore');
    }

    // Update the last tracked counts in localStorage
    localStorage.setItem('lastTrackedCasualCount', casualCount);
    localStorage.setItem('lastTrackedAvidCount', avidCount);
    localStorage.setItem('lastTrackedHardcoreCount', hardcoreCount);
}

// Run the check when the page loads
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    checkMedalCounts();
});
	
	// Function to track clicks on articles by publisher
function trackArticleClick(publisherName) {
    gtag('event', 'article_click', {
        'event_category': 'publisher_tracking',
        'event_label': publisherName, // The dynamic name of the publisher
        'value': 1 // Optional value for counting each click
    });
}

// Add event listener to all article links on page load
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    // Select all article links inside the rss-article-box class
    const articleLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.rss-article-box a');

    // Add click event listener to each article link
    articleLinks.forEach(link => {
        link.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
            // Find the closest article box to get the publisher name
            const articleBox = link.closest('.rss-article-box');
            if (articleBox) {
                // Retrieve the publisher's name from the span inside the rss-article-lower class
                const publisherSpan = articleBox.querySelector('.rss-article-lower .publisher-time-wrapper span');
                const publisherName = publisherSpan ? publisherSpan.textContent.trim() : 'Unknown Publisher';

                // Track the click with the publisher name
                trackArticleClick(publisherName);
            }
        });
    });
});

// Track the load more button
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    const loadMoreButton = document.getElementById('load-more-articles');

    if (loadMoreButton) {
        loadMoreButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
            // Send event to Google Analytics 4
            gtag('event', 'load_more', {
                event_category: 'engagement',
                event_label: 'Load More Articles',
                value: 1
            });
            console.log('Load more button clicked');
        });
    }
});


</script>

<script>
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
    // ✅ Hamburger Menu Toggle for Desktop (Uses Original Fullscreen Menu)
    $('#menu-toggle-desktop').on('click', function() {
        $(this).toggleClass('open');
        $('#fullscreen-menu').toggleClass('active');
    });

    // ✅ Clicking Medals or Progress Bar Opens Badge Popup
    $('#progress-bar-desktop, #top-right-medals').on('click', function() {
        $('#badge-popup').fadeIn();
    });
});
</script>
<script>
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {

    // Scroll Detection for Logo to Progress Bar Flip
    $(window).on('scroll', function() {
        if ($(window).scrollTop() > 70) {
            $('#flip-container').addClass('flipped');
        } else {
            $('#flip-container').removeClass('flipped');
        }
    });

    // Fetch WordPress Menu Items via AJAX
    function loadMenuItems() {
        $.ajax({
            url: '/wp-json/custom/v1/menu',
            method: 'GET',
            success: function(data) {
                let menuHTML = '';
                data.forEach(item => {
                    menuHTML += `<li><a href="${item.url}">${item.title}</a></li>`;
                });
                $('#dynamic-menu').html(menuHTML);  // For left menu
                $('#dynamic-menu2').html(menuHTML); // For right menu
                console.log("✅ Menu items loaded successfully.");
            },
            error: function() {
                console.error("❌ Failed to fetch menu items.");
            }
        });
    }
    loadMenuItems(); // Load the menus on page load


    // Function to disable page scrolling by fixing the body's position
    function disableScrolling() {
        const scrollY = window.scrollY;
        document.body.style.position = 'fixed';
        document.body.style.top = `-${scrollY}px`;
        document.body.style.width = '100%';
    }

    // Function to enable page scrolling and restore the previous scroll position
    function enableScrolling() {
        const scrollY = document.body.style.top;
        document.body.style.position = '';
        document.body.style.top = '';
        window.scrollTo(0, parseInt(scrollY || '0') * -1);
    }

    // Toggle Menu 1 (Left Menu)
    $('#menu-toggle').on('click', function() {
        $(this).toggleClass('open'); // Toggle the X animation for the hamburger icon
        $('#fullscreen-menu').toggleClass('active');
        if ($('#fullscreen-menu').hasClass('active')) {
            disableScrolling();
        } else {
            enableScrolling();
        }
    });

// Toggle Menu 2 (Right Data Icon Menu)
$('#menu-toggle2').on('click', function() {
    const svgIcon = $(this).find('.menu-icon');     // Your podium SVG
    const closeIcon = $(this).find('.close-icon');  // The "X" icon

    $('#fullscreen-menu2').toggleClass('active');

    if ($('#fullscreen-menu2').hasClass('active')) {
        svgIcon.hide();
        closeIcon.show();
        disableScrolling();

        // ✅ Trigger the event when the menu is activated
        document.dispatchEvent(new Event("fullscreenMenuOpened"));
    } else {
        svgIcon.show();
        closeIcon.hide();
        enableScrolling();
    }
});



    // Clicking Progress Bar Opens Badge Popup
    $('#progress-bar').on('click', function() {
        $('#badge-popup').fadeIn();
    });
});

//Navigating slides
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
    const slides = document.querySelectorAll('.css-slider .slide');
    const prevButton = document.querySelector('.nav-button.prev');
    const nextButton = document.querySelector('.nav-button.next');
    let currentIndex = 0;

    function showSlide(index) {
        slides.forEach((slide, i) => {
            slide.classList.remove('active');
            if (i === index) {
                slide.classList.add('active');
            }
        });
    }

    prevButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
        currentIndex = (currentIndex === 0) ? slides.length - 1 : currentIndex - 1;
        showSlide(currentIndex);
    });

    nextButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
        currentIndex = (currentIndex === slides.length - 1) ? 0 : currentIndex + 1;
        showSlide(currentIndex);
    });

    // Show the first slide initially
    showSlide(currentIndex);

    // Touch Swipe Handling
    let startX = 0;
    let endX = 0;

    document.getElementById('css-slider').addEventListener('touchstart', function(event) {
        startX = event.touches[0].clientX;
    });

    document.getElementById('css-slider').addEventListener('touchend', function(event) {
        endX = event.changedTouches[0].clientX;

        if (startX - endX > 50) { // Swipe Left
            nextButton.click();
        } else if (endX - startX > 50) { // Swipe Right
            prevButton.click();
        }
    });
});
	
	jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
    // Insert shortcode content into the divs
    $('#driver-monitor-content').html(shortcodeData.driverMonitor);
    $('#f1-standings-content').html(shortcodeData.f1Standings);
});


jQuery(document).ready(function($) {

    function refreshShortcodes() {
        console.log("🔄 Refreshing Shortcodes via AJAX");

        $.ajax({
            url: '/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php',
            type: 'POST',
            data: { action: 'render_shortcodes' },
            success: function(response) {
                console.log("✅ Raw AJAX Response: ", response);

                if (response) {
                    if (response.driverMonitor) {
                        console.log("✅ Driver Monitor Data Loaded Successfully.");
                        $('#driver-monitor-content').html(response.driverMonitor);
                    }

                    if (response.f1Standings) {
                        console.log("✅ F1 Standings Data Loaded Successfully.");
                        $('#f1-standings-content').html(response.f1Standings);
                    }

                    // Initialize Load More button handlers again after loading new content
                    initializeF1StandingsInteraction();
                } else {
                    console.error("❌ No Data Received from AJAX Response.");
                }
            },
            error: function(xhr, status, error) {
                console.error("❌ AJAX Request Failed:", status, error);
            }
        });
    }

    function initializeF1StandingsInteraction() {
        console.log("🔄 Re-initializing F1 Standings Interaction");

        $('.f1-standings').find('.toggle-drivers').off('click').on('click', function() {
            console.log("Drivers Load More Button Clicked");
            $(this).trigger('click');
        });

        $('.f1-standings').find('.toggle-constructors').off('click').on('click', function() {
            console.log("Constructors Load More Button Clicked");
            $(this).trigger('click');
        });
    }

    // Trigger refreshShortcodes only when needed
    $('#notification-button').on('click', function() {
        console.log("🔔 Notification Button Clicked.");
        refreshShortcodes();
    });

    document.addEventListener("fullscreenMenuOpened", function() {
        console.log("📂 Fullscreen Menu Opened. Loading Shortcodes...");
        refreshShortcodes();
    });

    // Initializing the tables only if the shortcodeData is present and not empty
    if (typeof shortcodeData !== 'undefined') {
        console.log("✅ Shortcode Data Found. Initializing Directly.");
        if (shortcodeData.driverMonitor) {
            $('#driver-monitor-content').html(shortcodeData.driverMonitor);
        }
        if (shortcodeData.f1Standings) {
            $('#f1-standings-content').html(shortcodeData.f1Standings);
        }
        initializeF1StandingsInteraction();
    } else {
        console.log("⚠️ No shortcodeData found. Triggering refreshShortcodes() instead.");
        refreshShortcodes();
    }
});




</script>

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Oscar Piastri arrived in Bahrain with unfinished b</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Oscar Piastri arrived in Bahrain with unfinished business. After looking like the 2025 title favourite and building a 34-point lead, his campaign bent at the worst time: the Azerbaijan crashes, then six races without a podium. McLaren’s read was consistent and specific, pointing to low-grip weekends where the car slid more and extracting lap time meant committing to understeer, oversteer and lock-ups rather than trying to tidy them away.

That’s why the chatter has returned as F1 heads into its 2026 reset. Early signs suggest smaller, lighter cars with less downforce and a lot more movement: snappy, sliding, and demanding patience on braking and traction. It could expose the same weakness again, or give Piastri a cleaner, more progressive kind of low grip that suits him better. With Norris now the reigning champion, the internal pressure is real, and 2026 may be decided by who stays fastest while the platform never fully settles.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Lando Norris gave a no-nonsense reply in Bahrain t</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Lando Norris gave a no-nonsense reply in Bahrain to Max Verstappen’s gloomy verdict on F1’s 2026 rules: if you don’t like it, nobody’s forcing you to stay. Norris said he’s enjoying the new-spec cars so far and reckons drivers can’t complain too loudly when the job is still driving the fastest cars in the world for huge money.

Verstappen, after piling on laps, branded the new era “anti-racing” and compared it to “Formula E on steroids” as F1 heads for a 50/50 electric and biofuel split with lighter cars and energy management at the centre. Norris admitted the cars don’t yet feel as quick or as polished, but backed the challenge and expects pace to come fast as teams develop them. And whatever Verstappen says now, Norris expects the same thing when it counts: Max will still go all-in to win.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Nigel Mansell has sounded an early warning on F1’s</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Nigel Mansell has sounded an early warning on F1’s 2026 reset: the new 50/50 split between electric and combustion power can’t turn racing into battery conservation. His fear is simple and visual — drivers lifting mid-lap, even in qualifying, because the numbers demand harvesting, not because they’re missing grip. For Mansell, the FIA’s priority is making sure it still looks and feels like flat-out racing.

Energy management is already the headline as the season opens, with new boost and overtake tools set to shape how battles unfold. Lando Norris expects more “yo-yoing” and chaos from mismatched deployment, while George Russell points to tiny harvesting gains becoming decisive. Mansell also backs Lewis Hamilton to bounce back at Ferrari if the car is right, and tips a three-team fight with Mercedes, McLaren and Ferrari in the mix. The tech may change everything, but the spectacle can’t afford to look hesitant.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Mercedes has rolled into the first 2026 pre-season</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Mercedes has rolled into the first 2026 pre-season test with a storm brewing around one word in the new power-unit rules: “ambient”. The compression ratio is capped at 16:1 when measured in ambient conditions, but paddock talk claims Mercedes has found a way for that figure to effectively climb once the engine is up to temperature, with rivals floating numbers as high as 18:1 and a potentially meaningful performance gain.

Ferrari, Audi, Honda and Red Bull Powertrains are pushing for a rewrite or new measurement method to close any “hot” advantage, and a supermajority vote could force a change regardless of Mercedes’ stance. Toto Wolff, meanwhile, has turned the spotlight elsewhere by calling Red Bull-Ford the early benchmark and even suggesting their energy deployment looks “a second a lap” better over consecutive runs — comments widely read as classic narrative management as F1’s first big 2026 governance fight takes shape.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Charles Leclerc set the pace on Day 2 in Bahrain a</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Charles Leclerc set the pace on Day 2 in Bahrain and nobody found a way past it. His 1:34.273 from the cooler morning session survived an afternoon defined by five red flags and broken-up run plans, while Ferrari quietly focused on detail work rather than theatrics, including more flow-vis checks as it kept Leclerc in the SF-26 all day.

Behind the headline time, the paddock’s mood was shaped by reliability and early trends: Mercedes lost most of the morning to an engine issue, Red Bull had a hydraulic leak that wiped out Isack Hadjar’s first session, and Aston Martin kept logging laps but sounded blunt about its deficit. The other talking point was Red Bull’s apparent Turn 1 advantage, with rivals already noting a consistent gain there. Add in Alpine’s late stoppage, Norris running dirty-air drills, and a few off-track moments, and it was a day of learning—just rarely uninterrupted.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Aston Martin’s AMR26 looks the part, but Lance Str</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Aston Martin’s AMR26 looks the part, but Lance Stroll’s Bahrain verdict was brutally clear: the car is around four to four-and-a-half seconds off the front and needs “four seconds of performance” to get into the fight. He pointed to a mix of engine, balance and grip issues, with braking and downshifts still “not great” as the new Honda power unit characteristics feed into the handling.

The bigger worry is time. A disrupted Barcelona test left Aston short on mileage, and Bahrain hasn’t been the clean reset they needed, with the gap on the timesheets underlining how much baseline work is still missing. Stroll kept it matter-of-fact, leaning on upgrades and steady progress rather than miracles before Melbourne, while Honda has also played down expectations despite insisting nothing is terminal.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Adrian Newey has cut through the politeness around</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Adrian Newey has cut through the politeness around F1’s latest 2026 flashpoint, admitting “I’m biased” as the sport argues over a compression-ratio rule that could shape the new power-unit era before it starts. The regulations cap geometric compression at 16:1 when measured at ambient temperature, but rivals believe Mercedes has found a way to achieve an effective 18:1 in real operating conditions.

Ferrari, Honda, Audi and Red Bull Powertrains want the policing changed to reflect how the engine behaves when hot, either via sensors on track or checks at operating temperature. Mercedes, led by Toto Wolff, insists it’s played it straight with the FIA kept closely informed, warning against moving the goalposts after designs are locked in — with customers McLaren, Williams and Alpine caught in the fallout. With a supermajority vote possible among manufacturers, FIA and FOM, this is heading toward Melbourne with politics firmly ahead of the racing.

The branding will appear on the FW48 (including halo and rear wing endplates), in Williams hospitality at European rounds, and on the helmets of both Sainz and Alex Albon, with extra placements on Sainz’s design reflecting how closely the relationship remains tied to the Spaniard.

The move lands after Williams’ one-season Santander stint ended, with Barclays set as the team’s banking partner for 2026. With an all-new rules era, a new Madrid race and two Spanish rounds on the calendar, the timing is no accident: Williams secures continuity around a marquee signing, while Estrella Galicia gains the scale of a team platform. Santander, meanwhile, stays in F1 via race sponsorship at eight events, including both Spanish GPs and all three US races.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Ferrari opened Thursday morning in Bahrain exactly</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Ferrari opened Thursday morning in Bahrain exactly how it wants to start this new 2026 era: quick, tidy and productive. Charles Leclerc topped the session with a 1:34.273, 0.511s clear of Lando Norris, while McLaren quietly impressed too by pairing pace with the most mileage (64 laps) as teams focus on learning these new cars as much as chasing headline times.

Further back, Pierre Gasly put Alpine third ahead of Oliver Bearman’s Haas and Alex Albon’s Williams, with Audi a touch lighter on running. The big talking points, though, were the interruptions: Mercedes lost almost the entire morning to a power unit issue for Kimi Antonelli (3 laps), while Red Bull’s hydraulic leak limited Isack Hadjar to a single late lap. After two mornings, Bahrain is already making reliability a performance metric of its own.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Ferrari topped Bahrain testing’s second morning wi</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Ferrari topped Bahrain testing’s second morning with Charles Leclerc, but the bigger headline was mileage. The SF26 looked settled enough to run hard and often: Leclerc set a 1:34.273 and logged 62 laps, while Lando Norris kept McLaren close on pure productivity too with 64 laps and a 1:34.784. In a fresh regs cycle, the early winners are the teams banking clean running, not just chasing one-off times.

The contrast was brutal for two heavyweights. Red Bull lost almost the entire session to a hydraulic leak and only managed a late installation lap for Isack Hadjar, while Mercedes saw Kimi Antonelli stopped after three laps by an engine issue. Elsewhere, Alpine, Haas and Williams quietly racked up full programmes, Cadillac recovered well from an early throttle problem, and Aston Martin continued the steady integration work with its new Honda power unit.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Toto Wolff rarely hands out public praise without </span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Toto Wolff rarely hands out public praise without a reason, but Bahrain testing has forced his clearest verdict yet: Red Bull’s 2026 package is the benchmark right now. Despite a Mercedes-powered McLaren topping day one, Wolff pointed to Red Bull’s straight-line performance and, crucially, its energy deployment as the standout — claiming it’s worth around a second a lap when repeated over consecutive laps.

Max Verstappen backed it up with 136 trouble-free laps, underlining the reliability and maturity of Red Bull Powertrains’ first on-track power unit, now in its sixth iteration and heading for FIA homologation. With Ford in the mix and a programme years in the making, Red Bull already looks like a composed manufacturer operation — and when asked if Mercedes can match it, Wolff’s answer was blunt: “Today, no.”

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Lewis Hamilton has delivered one of the first big </span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Lewis Hamilton has delivered one of the first big talking points of the 2026 era in Bahrain: F1 risks disappearing into its own complexity. With the new rules now on track — revised chassis and power units, and hybrids supplying 50% of total output — energy harvest and deployment sit closer to the heart of performance than ever, bringing software-led decisions that can be tough to translate for viewers.

Hamilton says the challenge behind the wheel may be manageable, but the concept is “ridiculously complex” for fans, especially with systems that learn a driver’s style and can be thrown off by a lock-up or running wide. For Ferrari, day one was about groundwork rather than fireworks: Leclerc and Hamilton logged 132 laps in a reliable run, with Leclerc third and Hamilton seventh. The mileage matters, but so does the story staying legible.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Mark Webber won’t be a constant trackside presence</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Mark Webber won’t be a constant trackside presence around Oscar Piastri in 2026, stepping back from the week-to-week paddock grind to focus more on the commercial and contractual side of Piastri’s programme. He isn’t leaving management duties with Ann Neal, but he’s expected to attend only select races across the 24-round season.

In his place at most grands prix will be a familiar ally: Pedro Matos, the race engineer who worked with Piastri during his ruthlessly efficient 2021 F2 title run. With Piastri coming off a 2025 campaign where he matched Lando Norris for wins but faded late as Norris took the championship, the reshuffle looks like a targeted upgrade to his weekend operation—adding trusted trackside support while keeping Webber’s experience in the background and maintaining continuity with sports psychologist Emma Murray.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">F1’s 2026 power unit rules are heading for a high-</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="F1’s 2026 power unit rules are heading for a high-stakes vote as homologation looms on March 1, with Mercedes at the centre of an argument over how compression ratio should be measured. The regs cap the geometric ratio at 16.0, but leave the test method to each manufacturer “at ambient temperature” for FIA approval. Rival paddock voices believe Mercedes HPP and Red Bull Powertrains may have used that wording to pass the ambient check while gaining a higher effective ratio when the engine runs hot, prompting calls for a new, hot-temperature compliance test.

The FIA says the PU Advisory Committee is discussing alignment on hot testing, and Red Bull is now understood to have joined Ferrari, Audi and Honda in pushing for it. With a supermajority (four of five PU makers) plus FIA and F1 approval, a late change could still be forced through—risking either protests and a season under a cloud if nothing changes, or a rushed new requirement that hits designs already locked in. Mercedes insists it stayed close to the FIA, believes it’s legal, and Toto Wolff says there’s no plan to sue—yet the process is already under strain before 2026 even arrives.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Lando Norris wasted no time stamping his authority</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Lando Norris wasted no time stamping his authority on F1’s new 2026 era, topping day one of the first official pre-season test in Bahrain. The reigning champion’s late 1:34.669 put McLaren P1, edging Max Verstappen by 0.129s after Red Bull had led much of the day and briefly regained the upper hand with a 1:34.830.

Behind them, Charles Leclerc ended third after taking over from Lewis Hamilton post-lunch, with Esteban Ocon an eye-catching fourth for Haas and Oscar Piastri keeping a second McLaren in the top five from the morning. Testing caveats remain, but the Norris-Verstappen rhythm is already back, amid red flags and reliability notes: Hulkenberg stopped on track for Audi, Aston Martin investigated a PU “data anomaly,” Racing Bulls ended early with a fluid leak, and Mercedes managed Antonelli’s reduced running while addressing a set-up issue.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Day one in Bahrain didn’t deliver answers so much </span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Day one in Bahrain didn’t deliver answers so much as a new pecking order of clues — and McLaren made the clearest statement. Lando Norris topped the opening times with a tidy 1:34.669 and 50 laps, the kind of clean, caveat-free headline that lands early. Oscar Piastri backed it up in P5 after his morning run, giving McLaren a drama-free, quietly authoritative start.

Red Bull took the other route: Max Verstappen piled on a class-leading 129 laps and finished just 0.129s off, showing a team more interested in executing the plan than chasing day-one glory. Ferrari began in pursuit mode — Charles Leclerc P3, Lewis Hamilton P7 — while Esteban Ocon’s P4 for Haas turned heads as an early “interesting” marker. Mercedes sat in the mix without threatening the top, and red flags for Alpine (Colapinto) and Audi (Hulkenberg) underlined how costly interruptions are when every test hour matters.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">F1’s second pre-season test of 2026 begins in Bahr</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="F1’s second pre-season test of 2026 begins in Bahrain on 11 February, but the first real look at the new-era cars comes with the doors half closed. Live broadcast access remains limited: local rights-holders can only show the final hour of running on each of the three days, plus a post-session highlights show, leaving the most revealing long stints largely out of sight.

All 10 teams are expected to be there after Williams missed the opening days in Barcelona, and Bahrain’s abrasive layout should stress new packages and tyre understanding early. Just remember what testing always is: programmes, fuel loads, masked engine modes and correlation work, where the cleanest day often matters more than the quickest lap. Full coverage returns for the final test on 18–20 February, when the picture finally opens up.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Mercedes is staring down a late-rule headache on i</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Mercedes is staring down a late-rule headache on its 2026 power unit as rivals push the FIA to tighten how the new compression-ratio limit is checked, just days before March 1 homologation locks designs in. The rule’s figure has already dropped from 18:1 to 16:1, and it’s currently defined by an ambient-temperature measurement. Now Honda, Audi and Ferrari are understood to be aligned with Red Bull Powertrains in lobbying for a “hot” running measurement that could effectively rewrite the practical limit.

The underlying claim is that Mercedes can meet the ambient test yet run a higher effective compression ratio once up to temperature, turning this into a fight over interpretation rather than outright legality. Toto Wolff says Mercedes won’t go legal even if the FIA backs a late clarification or change, but admits the timing could be damaging for Mercedes and its customer teams if a new method is voted through and can’t be met in time. The next few days are political as much as technical, with votes — not private assurances — set to decide who’s caught out.

			<span class="sbi-screenreader">Lewis Hamilton arrived in Bahrain focused on Ferra</span>
									<img width="1000" height="560" decoding="async" src="https://fastestlap.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="Lewis Hamilton arrived in Bahrain focused on Ferrari’s new car and the shifting rules landscape, but ended up flagging a more basic concern: stability on the radio. He confirmed Carlo Santi, who’s been in his ear during testing, is only a short-term fix and will stay for “a few races” before Ferrari switches again.

After a difficult 2025 learning curve and a public lack of chemistry with Riccardo Adami, another early-season engineer change is, in Hamilton’s words, “detrimental” — the kind of quiet disruption that can cost clarity, confidence and lap time when everyone’s already adapting. Ferrari hasn’t named a long-term replacement, with paddock speculation circling Cedric Michel-Grosjean, but the bigger issue is what the shuffle says about team organisation at a moment when every early point and every clean reference matters.

Oscar Piastri was a close second for McLaren (+0.169s), with George Russell third for Mercedes ahead of Lewis Hamilton’s first Ferrari test morning in fourth.

As ever, the stopwatch came with caveats, but mileage told its own story. Carlos Sainz topped the lap count with 77 for Williams, while rookie Arvid Lindblad impressed with 75 clean laps for Racing Bulls. Haas enjoyed a productive run in fifth with Esteban Ocon, Cadillac’s first official test ended solidly with Valtteri Bottas ninth, and Audi logged steady running with Gabriel Bortoleto in a B-spec car. Aston Martin had a quieter start, and Alpine’s morning was disrupted by a stoppage for Franco Colapinto that brought out the only red flag and limited his running.

<script>
(function() {
  function updateRaceCountdown() {
    const countdownEl = document.getElementById('race-countdown');
    if (!countdownEl) return false;

    const iso = countdownEl.getAttribute('data-days-remaining');
    if (!iso) return false;

    const raceDate = new Date(iso);
    if (isNaN(raceDate.getTime())) return false;

    const now   = new Date();
    const msDay = 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24;

    let daysLeft = Math.ceil((raceDate - now) / msDay);
    daysLeft = Math.max(0, daysLeft);

    let text;
    if (daysLeft === 0) text = 'Race day!';
    else if (daysLeft === 1) text = 'Tomorrow';
    else text = daysLeft + ' days to go';

    const daysSpan = document.getElementById('days-left');
    if (daysSpan) daysSpan.textContent = text;

    return true;
  }

  function boot() {
    // Try immediately…
    if (updateRaceCountdown()) return;

    // …then retry for up to ~3 seconds (covers late-injected markup).
    let tries = 0;
    const t = setInterval(() => {
      tries++;
      if (updateRaceCountdown() || tries >= 30) clearInterval(t);
    }, 100);
  }

  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', boot);
})();
</script>

        width: 100%; /* Full width on mobile */
    }

    .grid-lights {
        max-width: 300px; /* Ensure lights take full width on small screens */
    }
}
/* Logo container at the top of the game popup */
#popup-logo {
    position: relative;
    top: 10px; /* Adjust as needed for spacing */
    text-align: center;
    width: 100%; /* Full width inside its container */
    height: auto; /* Maintain aspect ratio */
    max-width: 250px; /* Optional: Limit the maximum width */
    display: block;

     margin-bottom: 20px;

        document.head.appendChild(style);
    });

<script>
    window.addEventListener('load', function() {
        // Show the game button after the page fully loads
        document.getElementById('game-toggle-button').style.display = 'block';

        // Share screenshot functionality
        const shareButton = document.getElementById('share-button');
        const nameInput = document.getElementById('name-input');
        const staticName = document.getElementById('static-name');

        // Sync the static div with the input value
        nameInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
            staticName.textContent = nameInput.value;
        });

        shareButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
            // Check if the name field is empty
            if (!nameInput.value.trim()) {
                nameInput.classList.add('error'); // Add red border for error
                alert('Please enter your name before sharing!');
                return;
            }

            // Remove the red error border if name is valid
            nameInput.classList.remove('error');

            // Elements to hide before taking the screenshot
            const elementsToHide = [
                document.getElementById('close-button'),
                document.getElementById('share-button'),
                document.getElementById('start-button'),
                document.getElementById('retry-button'),
                document.getElementById('reaction-button'),
                document.getElementById('result-placeholder'),
                nameInput // Add the input to the list of hidden elements
            ];

            // Show static name, hide the input
            staticName.style.display = 'block';
            nameInput.style.display = 'none';

            // Hide specific elements
            elementsToHide.forEach(element => {
                if (element) element.style.display = 'none';
            });

            // Take the screenshot using html2canvas
            html2canvas(document.getElementById('game-popup')).then(canvas => {
                // Convert canvas to a blob
                canvas.toBlob(blob => {
                    const imageUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);

                    // Check if Web Share API is supported
                    if (navigator.share) {
                        navigator.share({
                            title: 'My Reaction Time Score!',
                            text: `Check out my reaction time score in the game!`,
                            files: [new File([blob], 'score.png', { type: blob.type })],
                        }).then(() => {
                            console.log('Shared successfully!');
                        }).catch(err => {
                            console.error('Sharing failed', err);
                        });
                    } else {
                        // For desktops: Download the screenshot as a fallback
                        const link = document.createElement('a');
                        link.href = imageUrl;
                        link.download = 'reaction-time-score.png';
                        link.click();
                    }

                    // Restore the hidden elements after the screenshot is taken
                    elementsToHide.forEach(element => {
                        if (element) element.style.display = 'block';
                    });

                    // Hide the static name and show the input again
                    staticName.style.display = 'none';
                    nameInput.style.display = 'block';
                });
            });
        });
    });
</script>

<script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/html2canvas/1.4.1/html2canvas.min.js" defer></script>



<script>

window.addEventListener('load', function() {
        // Your inline JavaScript code goes here
    
let lights = document.querySelectorAll('.light');
let startButton = document.getElementById('start-button');
let retryButton = document.getElementById('retry-button');
let reactionTimeSpan = document.getElementById('reaction-time');
let resultPlaceholder = document.getElementById('result-placeholder');
let reactionButton = document.getElementById('reaction-button');
let countdownDisplay = document.getElementById('countdown');

let startTime;
let lightsGreen = false;
let gameActive = false; // Track if the game is running
let invalidated = false; // Track if jump start happened
let countdownInterval; // Store the countdown interval
let lightsGreenTimeout; // Store the green light random delay


// Hide the result-placeholder initially
resultPlaceholder.style.visibility = 'hidden'; 

function setRedLights() {
    lights.forEach(light => {
        light.style.backgroundColor = 'red';
    });
}

function setDarkRedLights() {
    lights.forEach(light => {
        light.style.backgroundColor = 'darkred';
    });
}

function goGreen() {
    if (invalidated) return;
    lights.forEach(light => {
        light.style.backgroundColor = 'green';
    });
    lightsGreen = true;
    startTime = performance.now();
}

function countdownToStart(callback) {
    let count = 3;
    countdownDisplay.textContent = count;
    countdownDisplay.style.visibility = 'visible'; // Show countdown when game starts

    countdownInterval = setInterval(() => {
        count--;
        countdownDisplay.textContent = count;
        if (count === 0) {
            clearInterval(countdownInterval); // Clear countdown interval
            countdownDisplay.textContent = ''; // Clear countdown
            countdownDisplay.style.visibility = 'hidden'; // Hide countdown once it's done

            // Clear any previous lightsGreenTimeout before setting a new one
            clearTimeout(lightsGreenTimeout);
            lightsGreenTimeout = setTimeout(callback, Math.random() * 5000); // Random delay for lights to turn green
        }
    }, 1000);
}

function stopCountdown() {
    clearInterval(countdownInterval);
    countdownDisplay.textContent = "Jump Start. Try again!"; // Persistent jump start message
    countdownDisplay.style.visibility = 'visible'; // Make sure the jump start message is visible
}

function startGame() {
    // Clear any existing intervals and timeouts from the previous game
    clearInterval(countdownInterval); // Clear previous countdown if any
    clearTimeout(lightsGreenTimeout); // Clear previous green light timeout if any

    setRedLights();
    reactionTimeSpan.textContent = "0.000"; // Reset reaction time
    resultPlaceholder.style.visibility = 'hidden'; // Hide the result placeholder when starting the game
    startButton.style.visibility = 'hidden'; // Hide without removing from layout
    retryButton.style.visibility = 'hidden'; // Hide retry button
    countdownDisplay.style.visibility = 'hidden'; // Hide the countdown when game restarts
    lightsGreen = false;
    invalidated = false;
    gameActive = true; // Mark game as active

    reactionButton.disabled = false; // Enable the reaction button
    countdownToStart(goGreen); // Start countdown to green light
}

function checkReaction() {
    if (!gameActive || invalidated) return; // No action if game hasn't started or a jump start happened

    if (lightsGreen) {
        let endTime = performance.now();
        let reactionTime = ((endTime - startTime) / 1000).toFixed(3);
        reactionTimeSpan.textContent = reactionTime;
        resultPlaceholder.style.visibility = 'visible'; // Show the result placeholder after a valid reaction
        retryButton.style.visibility = 'visible'; // Show retry button after game ends
        lightsGreen = false;
        gameActive = false; // End the game
        reactionButton.disabled = true; // Disable the reaction button

        // Call to handle and store the new reaction time in the table and localStorage
        handleNewReactionTime(parseFloat(reactionTime)); // Convert string to number for proper calculations
    } else {
        // Early press: stop countdown and show "Jump Start"
        invalidated = true;
        gameActive = false;
        stopCountdown();
        retryButton.style.visibility = 'visible'; // Show retry button after a jump start
        reactionButton.disabled = true; // Disable reaction button until retry
    }
}

startButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
    startGame();
});

retryButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
    // Reset and start the game immediately when pressing retry
    setDarkRedLights();
    countdownDisplay.textContent = '';
    lightsGreen = false;
    invalidated = false;
    reactionButton.disabled = false; // Ensure the button is re-enabled properly
    startGame(); // Start the game immediately
    retryButton.style.visibility = 'hidden'; // Hide retry button again when restarting the game
});

reactionButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
    checkReaction();
});

// Set the pro reaction time to 0.250 seconds
const PRO_REACTION_TIME = 0.250;

// Initialize values from localStorage or defaults
let times = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('reactionTimes')) || []; // Array of reaction times
let latestTime = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('latestTime')) || 0.000; // Latest reaction time
let fastestTime = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('fastestTime')) || 0.000; // Fastest time stored
let averageTime = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('averageTime')) || 0.000; // Average of last 10 runs

// Update the table with saved values when the page loads
document.getElementById('last-time').textContent = latestTime.toFixed(3) + 's'; // Add 's' after the last-time
document.getElementById('avg-time').textContent = averageTime.toFixed(3) + 's'; // Add 's' after the avg-time
document.getElementById('fastest-time').textContent = fastestTime.toFixed(3) + 's'; // Add 's' after the fastest-time

function updateProTime(newTime) {
    const proTimeCell = document.getElementById('pro-time');
    let timeDifference = newTime - PRO_REACTION_TIME;

    if (timeDifference < 0) {
        proTimeCell.textContent = `-${Math.abs(timeDifference).toFixed(3)}s`;
        proTimeCell.style.color = '#A45EE5'; // Purple for faster than pro
    } else if (timeDifference === 0) {
        proTimeCell.textContent = '0.000';
        proTimeCell.style.color = '#A45EE5'; // Purple for matching pro time
    } else {
        proTimeCell.textContent = `+${timeDifference.toFixed(3)}s`;
        proTimeCell.style.color = '#FFD700'; // Yellow for slower than pro
    }
}

function updateTable(newTime) {
    // Update the latest run time (Column 1)
    latestTime = newTime;
    document.getElementById('last-time').textContent = latestTime.toFixed(3) + 's'; // Add 's' after the time
    localStorage.setItem('latestTime', latestTime); // Store in localStorage

    // Update the list of reaction times and average (Column 2)
    times.push(newTime);
    if (times.length > 10) {
        times.shift(); // Keep only the last 10 runs
    }
    averageTime = times.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / times.length;
    document.getElementById('avg-time').textContent = averageTime.toFixed(3) + 's'; // Add 's' after the average time
    localStorage.setItem('averageTime', averageTime); // Store average in localStorage
    localStorage.setItem('reactionTimes', JSON.stringify(times)); // Store all times

    // Update the fastest run time (Column 3)
    if (!fastestTime || newTime < fastestTime) {
        fastestTime = newTime;
        document.getElementById('fastest-time').textContent = fastestTime.toFixed(3) + 's'; // Add 's' after the fastest time
        localStorage.setItem('fastestTime', fastestTime); // Store in localStorage
    }

    // Update Pro Reaction Time (Column 4)
    updateProTime(newTime);
}

// Call this function after each run, passing the new reaction time
function handleNewReactionTime(newTime) {
    updateTable(newTime);
}
});

</script>



<script>
window.addEventListener('load', function() {
    // Prevent multi-touch gestures like pinch-to-zoom
    document.addEventListener('touchstart', function(event) {
        if (event.touches.length > 1) {
            event.preventDefault();
        }
    }, { passive: false });

    // Prevent double-tap zoom
    let lastTouchEnd = 0;
    document.addEventListener('touchend', function(event) {
        let now = (new Date()).getTime();
        if (now - lastTouchEnd <= 500) {
            event.preventDefault();
        }
        lastTouchEnd = now;
    }, false);

    // Toggle popup and scroll behavior
    const gameButton = document.getElementById('game-toggle-button');
    const buttonText = document.getElementById('button-text');
    const buttonIcon = gameButton.querySelector('i');
    const gamePopup = document.getElementById('game-popup'); // Assuming the popup has the id 'game-popup'

    // Function to disable page scrolling by fixing the body's position
    function disableScrolling() {
        const scrollY = window.scrollY;
        document.body.style.position = 'fixed';
        document.body.style.top = `-${scrollY}px`;
        document.body.style.width = '100%';
        preventPullToRefresh(); // Also prevent pull-to-refresh
    }

    // Function to enable page scrolling and restore the previous scroll position
    function enableScrolling() {
        const scrollY = document.body.style.top;
        document.body.style.position = '';
        document.body.style.top = '';
        window.scrollTo(0, parseInt(scrollY || '0') * -1);
        allowPullToRefresh(); // Re-enable pull-to-refresh
    }

    // Function to prevent pull-to-refresh gesture
    function preventPullToRefresh() {
        window.addEventListener('touchmove', preventDefault, { passive: false });
    }

    // Function to allow pull-to-refresh gesture again
    function allowPullToRefresh() {
        window.removeEventListener('touchmove', preventDefault);
    }

    // Prevent default behavior for touchmove
    function preventDefault(event) {
        if (event.touches.length > 1) {
            // Allow default behavior for multi-touch gestures
            return;
        }
        event.preventDefault();
    }

    gameButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
        if (gameButton.classList.contains('close-mode')) {
            // Switch to "Play the game" mode
            gameButton.classList.remove('close-mode');
            buttonText.textContent = 'Play the game';
            buttonIcon.className = 'fa-solid fa-gauge';
            
            // Close the game popup
            gamePopup.style.display = 'none';

            // Enable page scrolling when the game is closed
            enableScrolling();
        } else {
            // Switch to "Close game" mode
            gameButton.classList.add('close-mode');
            buttonText.textContent = ''; // Remove the text
            buttonIcon.className = 'fa-solid fa-x'; // Only show the X icon
            
            // Open the game popup
            gamePopup.style.display = 'flex'; // or 'block' depending on how you want it to appear

            // Disable page scrolling when the game is open
            disableScrolling();
        }
    });
});

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    // Ensure the nameInput and staticName exist
    const nameInput = document.getElementById('name-input');
    const staticName = document.getElementById('static-name');

    if (!nameInput || !staticName) {
        console.error('nameInput or staticName element not found.');
        return;
    }

    // Retrieve stored name from localStorage
    const storedName = localStorage.getItem('userName');
    if (storedName) {
        console.log('Retrieved stored name:', storedName);
        nameInput.value = storedName; // Pre-fill the input field with the stored name
        staticName.textContent = storedName; // Sync the static div
    }

    // Update localStorage and static div as the user types
    nameInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
        const inputName = nameInput.value;
        console.log('Updating name in localStorage:', inputName);
        localStorage.setItem('userName', inputName); // Store the name in localStorage
        staticName.textContent = inputName; // Sync static div
    });
});
</script>

<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    console.log("✅ JavaScript file loaded successfully.");

    function initializeStandings(container) {
        const teamColors = {
            'Mercedes': '#00D2BE',
            'Red Bull': '#1E41FF',
            'Ferrari': '#DC0000',
            'Aston Martin': '#008000',
            'McLaren': '#F98E1D',
            'Alpine F1 Team': '#2293D1',
            'RB F1 Team': '#4E7C9B',
            'Sauber': '#B12039',
            'Williams': '#37BEDD',
            'Haas': '#B6BABD'
        };

        function abbreviateName(name) {
            return name.substring(0, 3).toUpperCase();
        }

        function toggleRows(button, tableSelector) {
            const rows = container.querySelectorAll(`${tableSelector} .hidden-row`);
            const isExpanded = button.getAttribute("data-expanded") === "true";
            
            rows.forEach(row => row.style.display = isExpanded ? "none" : "table-row");
            button.textContent = isExpanded ? "LOAD MORE" : "LOAD LESS";
            button.setAttribute("data-expanded", isExpanded ? "false" : "true");
        }

        function populateTable(data, tableBodyClass, isDriverTable = true) {
            const tableBody = container.querySelector(`.${tableBodyClass}`);
            tableBody.innerHTML = "";

            data.forEach((item, index) => {
                const team = isDriverTable ? item.Constructors[0].name : item.Constructor.name;
                const teamColor = teamColors[team] || "#FFFFFF";
                const row = document.createElement("tr");
                row.className = index >= 5 ? "hidden-row" : "";
                row.style.backgroundColor = index % 2 === 0 ? "rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1)" : "rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.05)";
                const positionValue = item.position ? item.position : "-";

                row.innerHTML = `
                    <td class="pos">${positionValue}</td>
                    <td class="name" style="color: ${teamColor}; font-weight: bold;">
                        ${isDriverTable ? abbreviateName(item.Driver.familyName) : abbreviateName(item.Constructor.name)}
                    </td>
                    <td class="points">${item.points}</td>
                `;
                tableBody.appendChild(row);
            });
        }

        // Tab switching
        container.querySelectorAll(".tab-button").forEach(button => {
            button.addEventListener("click", function() {
                container.querySelectorAll(".tab-button").forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove("active"));
                container.querySelectorAll(".standings-tab").forEach(tab => tab.classList.remove("active"));

                this.classList.add("active");
                container.querySelector(`.${this.dataset.tab}`).classList.add("active");
            });
        });

        // Bind toggle buttons for "Load More"
        container.querySelectorAll(".toggle-drivers").forEach(button => {
            button.addEventListener("click", function() {
                toggleRows(this, ".drivers-body");
            });
        });
        container.querySelectorAll(".toggle-constructors").forEach(button => {
            button.addEventListener("click", function() {
                toggleRows(this, ".constructors-body");
            });
        });

        // Fetch the cached standings from the WordPress backend
        fetch(rss_ajax.ajax_url + '?action=get_f1_standings')
            .then(response => response.json())
            .then(result => {
                if (result.success && result.data) {
                    populateTable(result.data.drivers, "drivers-body", true);
                    populateTable(result.data.constructors, "constructors-body", false);
                } else {
                    console.error("No cached data available from backend.");
                }
            })
            .catch(error => console.error("Error fetching cached standings:", error));
    }

    // Initialize standings containers on page load
    document.querySelectorAll(".f1-standings-container").forEach(container => {
        initializeStandings(container);
        container.dataset.initialized = "true";  // Mark as initialized
    });

    // Re-initialize tables on mobile when the full-screen menu is opened
    document.addEventListener("fullscreenMenuOpened", function() {
        document.querySelectorAll(".f1-standings-container").forEach(container => {
            if (!container.dataset.initialized) {
                initializeStandings(container);
                container.dataset.initialized = "true";
            }
        });
    });

    // Hourly refresh on Sundays from the cached data (if needed)
    setInterval(() => {
        const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US', { weekday: 'long' });
        if (today === "Sunday") {
            console.log("🔄 Refreshing standings from cache...");
            document.querySelectorAll(".f1-standings-container").forEach(container => {
                fetch(rss_ajax.ajax_url + '?action=get_f1_standings')
                    .then(response => response.json())
                    .then(result => {
                        if (result.success && result.data) {
                            populateTable(result.data.drivers, "drivers-body", true);
                            populateTable(result.data.constructors, "constructors-body", false);
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(error => console.error("Error refreshing cached standings:", error));
            });
        }
    }, 60 * 60 * 1000); // Check every hour on Sundays

    // AJAX connectivity test
    fetch(rss_ajax.ajax_url + '?action=refresh_f1_standings')
        .then(response => response.json())
        .then(data => {
            console.log("✅ AJAX Test Response:", data);
        })
        .catch(error => {
            console.error("❌ AJAX Test Error:", error);
        });
});
</script>

    <script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function($) {

        function loadShortcodes(instanceId) {
            $.ajax({
                url: 'https://fastestlap.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php',
                type: 'POST',
                data: {
                    action: 'refresh_driver_monitor',
                    instance_id: instanceId
                },
                success: function(response) {
                    if (response.success) {
                        const driversHtml = response.data.drivers.map(driver => `
                            <div class="f1-monitor-row">
                                <div class="f1-monitor-info">
                                    <span class="f1-monitor-name">${driver.abbr}</span>
                                    <div class="f1-monitor-bar">
                                        <div style="width: ${(driver.percentage / response.data.max) * 100}%;"></div>
                                    </div>
                                    <span class="f1-monitor-percentage">${driver.percentage}%</span>
                                </div>
                                <span class="f1-monitor-sentiment ${driver.sentiment.toLowerCase()}">${driver.sentiment}</span>
                            </div>
                        `).join('');

                        // 🔹 Only update the rows, not the entire container
                        const targetContainer = $(`[data-instance-id="${response.data.instance_id}"]`);
                        targetContainer.find('.f1-monitor-rows').html(driversHtml);
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        // Initialize all plugin instances on the page
        $('[data-instance-id]').each(function() {
            const instanceId = $(this).data('instance-id');
            loadShortcodes(instanceId);
        });

    });
    </script>

<!-- HFCM by 99 Robots - Snippet # 7040: Swiper Cards Autoplay JS -->
<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    console.log("DOM fully loaded. Attaching autoplay handlers to existing Swiper instance.");

    let swiper;
    let autoplayInterval = null;
    let userInteracting = false;
    let interactionTimeout = null;
    let countdownAnimationFrame = null; // Track animation frame
    let direction = 1; // 1 for forward, -1 for backward
    const countdownDuration = 3000; // 3 seconds

    // Function to initialize/reinitialize the countdown circle
    function reinitializeCountdown() {
        console.log("Reinitializing countdown circle...");
        const existingCircle = document.querySelector(".countdown-circle");
        if (existingCircle) existingCircle.remove();

        const countdownCircle = document.createElement("div");
        countdownCircle.classList.add("countdown-circle");
        countdownCircle.innerHTML = `<span class="countdown-number">${(countdownDuration / 1000).toFixed(0)}</span>`;
        document.querySelector("#newsSwiper").appendChild(countdownCircle);
    }

    // Function to start the countdown animation
    function startCountdownAnimation() {
        const countdownCircle = document.querySelector(".countdown-circle");
        const countdownNumber = countdownCircle.querySelector(".countdown-number");
			   const duration = countdownDuration; // Total countdown duration in ms
        const startTime = performance.now();

        // Cancel any ongoing animation
        if (countdownAnimationFrame) {
            cancelAnimationFrame(countdownAnimationFrame);
        }

        function updateCountdown(currentTime) {
            const elapsed = currentTime - startTime;
        const remaining = Math.max(0, duration - elapsed); // Remaining time in ms
        const progress = remaining / duration;

            // Update circle progress and number
        countdownCircle.style.setProperty("--progress-percent", `${progress * 100}%`);
        countdownNumber.textContent = Math.ceil(remaining / 1000); // Show whole seconds

        if (elapsed < duration) {
            countdownAnimationFrame = requestAnimationFrame(updateCountdown);
        } else {
            countdownNumber.textContent = "0"; // Final value
        }
    }

    countdownAnimationFrame = requestAnimationFrame(updateCountdown);
}

    // Start autoplay with countdown
    function startAutoplay() {
        console.log("Starting autoplay...");
        clearInterval(autoplayInterval);
        reinitializeCountdown();
        startCountdownAnimation();

        autoplayInterval = setInterval(() => {
            if (!userInteracting) {
                const activeIndex = swiper.activeIndex;
                const totalSlides = swiper.slides.length;

                if (activeIndex === 0 && direction === -1) {
                    direction = 1; // Change to forward direction
                } else if (activeIndex === totalSlides - 1 && direction === 1) {
                    direction = -1; // Change to backward direction
                }

                if (direction === 1) {
                    swiper.slideNext();
                } else {
                    swiper.slidePrev();
                }

                console.log(`Navigating to slide ${swiper.activeIndex} in direction: ${direction === 1 ? "forward" : "backward"}`);
                reinitializeCountdown(); // Reset countdown after slide change
                startCountdownAnimation();
            }
        }, countdownDuration); // Match countdown duration
    }

    // Stop autoplay
    function stopAutoplay() {
        console.log("Stopping autoplay...");
        clearInterval(autoplayInterval);
        autoplayInterval = null;

        // Cancel any ongoing countdown animation
        if (countdownAnimationFrame) {
            cancelAnimationFrame(countdownAnimationFrame);
            countdownAnimationFrame = null;
        }
    }

    // Handle user interaction
    function handleUserInteraction() {
        console.log("User interacting. Stopping autoplay and animation...");
        userInteracting = true;
        stopAutoplay();

        clearTimeout(interactionTimeout);
        interactionTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
            console.log("Resuming autoplay after user interaction...");
            userInteracting = false;

            // Resume autoplay and countdown
            reinitializeCountdown();
            startAutoplay();
        }, 2000); // Resume autoplay after 2 seconds
    }

    // Initialize Swiper
    function initializeSwiper() {
        console.log("Initializing Swiper...");
        const swiperContainer = document.querySelector("#newsSwiper");

        if (!swiperContainer || !swiperContainer.swiper) {
            console.error("Swiper instance not found. Make sure Swiper is initialized before this script runs.");
            return;
        }

        swiper = swiperContainer.swiper;
			
			  // Ensure transition duration and easing for mobile and desktop consistency
    swiper.params.speed = 600; // 600ms transition duration
    swiper.params.easing = "ease-in-out"; // Smooth easing for transitions
    swiper.update(); // Apply updated settings

        swiper.on("touchStart", handleUserInteraction);
        swiper.on("touchEnd", handleUserInteraction);

        // Reset countdown animation after slide transition
        swiper.on("slideChangeTransitionEnd", function () {
            console.log("Slide transition ended. Resetting countdown...");
            reinitializeCountdown();
            startCountdownAnimation();
        });
    }

    // Handle refresh button click to reinitialize Swiper and countdown
    function handleUpdates() {
        const refreshButton = document.querySelector("#refresh-button");
        refreshButton.addEventListener("click", function () {
            console.log("Refresh button clicked, reinitializing Swiper and countdown...");
            setTimeout(() => {
                console.log("Reinitializing Swiper and countdown logic...");
                initializeSwiper();
                startAutoplay();
            }, 500); // Align with AJAX update timing
        });
    }

    // Handle visibility changes
    document.addEventListener("visibilitychange", function () {
        if (document.visibilityState === "visible") {
            console.log("Page visible. Resuming autoplay...");
            startAutoplay();
        } else {
            console.log("Page hidden. Stopping autoplay...");
            stopAutoplay();
        }
    });

    // Handle window focus and blur
    window.addEventListener("focus", startAutoplay);
    window.addEventListener("blur", stopAutoplay);

    initializeSwiper();
    startAutoplay();
    handleUpdates();
});



</script>


<style>
.countdown-circle {
    position: absolute;
    bottom: 16px;
    right: 16px;
    width: 50px;
    height: 50px;
    background: conic-gradient(
        #dd3333 0%,
        #007aff var(--progress-percent, 100%),
        rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1) var(--progress-percent, 100%),
        rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1) 100%
    );
    border-radius: 50%;
    z-index: 10;
    pointer-events: none; /* Prevent user interaction */
    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    color: #fff; /* Text color inside the circle */
    font-weight: bold;
    font-size: 14px;
}

</style>
