<!-- HFCM by 99 Robots - Snippet # 7044: Badge System JS -->
<script>
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {

    // ========= UTILITY FUNCTIONS ========= //
    
    // Returns the current date string (without time) for consistent comparisons.
    function getCurrentDateStr() {
        // produce "2025-04-20"
        return new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
    }

    // ========= GLOBAL VARIABLES ========= //
    
    // Load stored values or default to 0
    var currentScore       = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('currentScore')) || 0,
        totalArticlesClicked = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('totalArticlesClicked')) || 0,
        streak             = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('streak')) || 0,
        highestStreak      = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('highestStreak')) || 0,
        lastInteractionDateStr = localStorage.getItem('lastInteractionDate') || "";
    
    // Maximum score value; adjust as needed.
    var maxActions = 100;
    
    // Medal image URLs and associated class names
    var medalImages = {
        bronze: 'https://t0cd9jv7t2-staging.onrocket.site/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/bronze-medal.png',
        silver: 'https://t0cd9jv7t2-staging.onrocket.site/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/silver-medal.png',
        gold:   'https://t0cd9jv7t2-staging.onrocket.site/wp-content/uploads/2024/09/gold-medal-1.png'
    };

    // ========= UI & LOGIC FUNCTIONS ========= //

    // Updates the level text, medal icon display, and progress bar.
    function updateLevelDisplay() {
        var level = 'bronze';
        if (currentScore >= 100) {
            level = 'gold';
        } else if (currentScore >= 50) {
            level = 'silver';
        }
        
        // Define color and name schemes for the different levels.
        var colors = { bronze: '#cd7f32', silver: '#c0c0c0', gold: '#ffd700' },
            levelNames = { bronze: 'Casual Fan', silver: 'Serious Fan', gold: 'Hardcore Fan' };

        // Update the text and styling in the UI.
        $('#level-text').css('color', colors[level]).text(levelNames[level]);
        $('#overall-level-text').css('color', colors[level]).text(levelNames[level]);
        $('#overall-level-medal-svg').html('<img src="' + medalImages[level] + '" alt="' + levelNames[level] + '">');

        // Update the progress bar fill.
        var percentage = (currentScore / maxActions) * 100;
        $('.progress-bar-fill').css('width', percentage + '%');
			  $('.progress-bar-percentage').text(Math.round(percentage) + '%');


        // Hide all medal icons and then show only the appropriate one.
        $('#bronze-medal, #silver-medal, #gold-medal').hide();
        $('#' + level + '-medal').show();

        // Save the score.
        localStorage.setItem('currentScore', currentScore);
    }

    // Updates the counts in the popup (medal counts and article count).
    function updatePopupData() {
        $('#casual-fan-count').text(localStorage.getItem('casualFanCount') || 0);
        $('#avid-fan-count').text(localStorage.getItem('avidFanCount') || 0);
        $('#hardcore-fan-count').text(localStorage.getItem('hardcoreFanCount') || 0);
        $('#total-articles-count').text(totalArticlesClicked);
        updateLevelDisplay();
    }

    // Increases the current score (capped at maxActions) and updates the UI.
    function increaseScore(points) {
        currentScore = Math.min(currentScore + points, maxActions);
        updateLevelDisplay();
    }

    // Awards medals based on the previous day's score and stores medal counts.
    function awardMedalsAndUpdateStreak(previousScore) {
        var medalCounts = {
            hardcoreFanCount: parseInt(localStorage.getItem('hardcoreFanCount')) || 0,
            avidFanCount:     parseInt(localStorage.getItem('avidFanCount')) || 0,
            casualFanCount:   parseInt(localStorage.getItem('casualFanCount')) || 0
        };

        // Award medal based on the score.
        if (previousScore >= 100) {
            medalCounts.hardcoreFanCount++;
            console.log("Awarded gold medal. Total gold medals:", medalCounts.hardcoreFanCount);
        } else if (previousScore >= 50) {
            medalCounts.avidFanCount++;
            console.log("Awarded silver medal. Total silver medals:", medalCounts.avidFanCount);
        } else if (previousScore >= 10) {
            medalCounts.casualFanCount++;
            console.log("Awarded bronze medal. Total bronze medals:", medalCounts.casualFanCount);
        }
        localStorage.setItem('hardcoreFanCount', medalCounts.hardcoreFanCount);
        localStorage.setItem('avidFanCount', medalCounts.avidFanCount);
        localStorage.setItem('casualFanCount', medalCounts.casualFanCount);
    }

    // Checks if it is a new day. If so, awards medals, resets the score,
    // updates streak and stores the last reset date.
function resetDailyScoresIfNewDay() {
  const currentDateStr  = getCurrentDateStr();
  const storedResetDate = localStorage.getItem('lastResetDate')       || "";
  const storedInteract  = localStorage.getItem('lastInteractionDate') || "";

  // if it’s already been reset today, bail out
  if (storedResetDate === currentDateStr) return;

  console.log("New day detected. Resetting daily score and evaluating streak.");

  // 1) award medals for yesterday’s score
  const prevScore = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('currentScore')) || 0;
  awardMedalsAndUpdateStreak(prevScore);

  // 2) reset today’s score
  currentScore = 0;
  localStorage.setItem('lastResetDate',       getCurrentDateStr());
  localStorage.setItem('lastInteractionDate',  getCurrentDateStr());

  // 3) compute how many days since last interaction
  let newStreak = 1;
  if (storedInteract) {
    let lastDate = new Date(storedInteract);
    let today    = new Date();
    // strip times
    lastDate.setHours(0,0,0,0);
    today.setHours(0,0,0,0);

    const msPerDay = 1000*60*60*24;
    const diffDays = Math.round((today - lastDate)/msPerDay);

    if (diffDays === 1) {
      newStreak = (parseInt(localStorage.getItem('streak')) || 0) + 1;
    }
  }

  streak = newStreak;

  // 4) update highestStreak if needed
  if (streak > (parseInt(localStorage.getItem('highestStreak'))||0)) {
    highestStreak = streak;
    localStorage.setItem('highestStreak', highestStreak);
  }

  // 5) persist and also update lastInteractionDate
  localStorage.setItem('streak',                streak);
  localStorage.setItem('lastInteractionDate',   currentDateStr);

  console.log(`Streak is now ${streak}, highestStreak ${highestStreak}`);
}




    // Updates the streak display in the UI.
    function updateStreakUI() {
        $('#streak-count').text(streak);
        $('#highest-streak-count').text(highestStreak);
    }

    // Schedules an automatic reset at midnight.
    function resetScoresAtMidnight() {
        var now = new Date(),
            midnight = new Date();
        midnight.setHours(24, 0, 0, 0); // Set time to midnight
        var timeUntilMidnight = midnight - now;
        setTimeout(function() {
            resetDailyScoresIfNewDay();
            updateLevelDisplay();
            updatePopupData();
            updateStreakUI();
            // Schedule the next reset.
            resetScoresAtMidnight();
        }, timeUntilMidnight);
    }
    
    // ========= EVENT HANDLERS ========= //

    // Notification button click: Check for daily reset then increase score and update UI.
    $('#notification-popup').on('click', function() {
        resetDailyScoresIfNewDay();
        increaseScore(10);
        updatePopupData();
        updateStreakUI();
    });

    // When an article is clicked.
    $(document).on('click', 'a.rss-article-box', function() {
        var lastArticleClickTime = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('lastArticleClickTime')) || 0,
            currentTime = new Date().getTime();
        if (currentTime - lastArticleClickTime >= 20000) {
            totalArticlesClicked++;
            localStorage.setItem('totalArticlesClicked', totalArticlesClicked);
            increaseScore(10);
            updatePopupData();
            localStorage.setItem('lastArticleClickTime', currentTime);
        } else {
            console.log("Article click cooldown active. Please wait.");
        }
    });

    // When the "Load More Articles" button is clicked.
    $('#load-more-articles').on('click', function() {
        var lastLoadMoreTime = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('lastLoadMoreTime')) || 0,
            currentTime = new Date().getTime();
        if (currentTime - lastLoadMoreTime >= 5000) {
            increaseScore(5);
            localStorage.setItem('lastLoadMoreTime', currentTime);
        } else {
            console.log("Load More cooldown active.");
        }
    });
    
    // Open medal/score popup when the medal image is clicked.
    $('#top-right-medals img').on('click', function(e) {
        e.stopPropagation();
        $('#badge-popup').fadeIn();
    });
    // Close popup when the close button is clicked.
    $('.close-popup').on('click', function(e) {
        e.stopPropagation();
        $('#badge-popup').fadeOut();
    });
    
    // ========= INITIALIZATION ========= //

    // Run the daily check and update the UI immediately.
    resetDailyScoresIfNewDay();
    updateStreakUI();
    updateLevelDisplay();
    updatePopupData();
    
    // Schedule the automatic reset at midnight.
    resetScoresAtMidnight();

});
</script>

<!-- /end HFCM by 99 Robots -->
<!-- HFCM by 99 Robots - Snippet # 7045: Swipe gesture JS -->
<script>
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
    console.log("🚀 Slide System Initialized");

    const slides = document.querySelectorAll('#css-slider .slide');
    const prevButton = document.querySelector('.nav-button.prev');
    const nextButton = document.querySelector('.nav-button.next');
    const sliderContainer = document.querySelector('#fullscreen-menu2');
    const sliderContent = document.querySelector('#slider-container');
    const tables = document.querySelectorAll('.f1-standings, .f1-monitor-container');
    let currentIndex = 0;
    let startX = 0;
    let startY = 0;
    let endX = 0;
    let endY = 0;
    let isSwiping = false;
    let isVerticalScroll = false;
    let isScrollPaused = false;
    let scrollTimeout;

    if (slides.length === 0) {
        console.error("❌ No slides found. Please check your slide HTML structure.");
        return;
    }

    console.log(`📊 Total Slides Found: ${slides.length}`);

    function showSlide(index) {
        slides.forEach((slide, i) => {
            slide.classList.remove('active');
            slide.style.display = (i === index) ? "block" : "none";
        });
    }

    showSlide(currentIndex);

    function changeSlide(direction) {
        if (isScrollPaused) return;

        if (direction === 'next') {
            currentIndex = (currentIndex === slides.length - 1) ? 0 : currentIndex + 1;
        } else if (direction === 'prev') {
            currentIndex = (currentIndex === 0) ? slides.length - 1 : currentIndex - 1;
        }
        showSlide(currentIndex);
    }

    if (prevButton) {
        prevButton.addEventListener('click', () => changeSlide('prev'));
    }

    if (nextButton) {
        nextButton.addEventListener('click', () => changeSlide('next'));
    }

    function handleTouchStart(event) {
        if (event.touches.length === 1) {
            const targetElement = event.target;

            startX = event.touches[0].clientX;
            startY = event.touches[0].clientY;
            endX = startX;
            endY = startY;
            isSwiping = true;
            isVerticalScroll = false;
        }
    }

    function handleTouchMove(event) {
        if (isSwiping) {
            endX = event.touches[0].clientX;
            endY = event.touches[0].clientY;

            const diffX = Math.abs(endX - startX);
            const diffY = Math.abs(endY - startY);

            if (diffY > diffX && diffY > 10) {
                isVerticalScroll = true;
                isSwiping = false;

                clearTimeout(scrollTimeout);
                isScrollPaused = true;

                scrollTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
                    isScrollPaused = false;
                }, 400);
            }
        }
    }

    function handleTouchEnd() {
        if (!isSwiping || isVerticalScroll || isScrollPaused) return;

        const diffX = startX - endX;

        if (Math.abs(diffX) > 50) {
            if (diffX > 0) {
                changeSlide('next');
            } else {
                changeSlide('prev');
            }
        }
        isSwiping = false;
    }

    tables.forEach(table => {
        table.addEventListener('touchstart', function(event) {
            handleTouchStart(event);
            event.stopPropagation(); // 🚫 Prevents propagation to outer handlers
        });

        table.addEventListener('touchmove', function(event) {
            handleTouchMove(event);
            event.stopPropagation(); // 🚫 Prevents propagation to outer handlers
        });

        table.addEventListener('touchend', function(event) {
            handleTouchEnd();
            event.stopPropagation(); // 🚫 Prevents propagation to outer handlers
        });
    });

    sliderContainer.addEventListener('touchstart', handleTouchStart);
    sliderContainer.addEventListener('touchmove', handleTouchMove);
    sliderContainer.addEventListener('touchend', handleTouchEnd);

    console.log("✅ Swipe Gesture Handling Successfully Initialized.");
});
</script>

<!-- /end HFCM by 99 Robots -->
<!-- HFCM by 99 Robots - Snippet # 7046: New Tab for Desktop links -->
<script>
  jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
    function isMobileOrTablet() {
      return /Mobi|Android|iPhone|iPad|iPod/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
    }

    if (!isMobileOrTablet()) {
      $(document).on('click', 'a', function(e) {
        var href = $(this).attr('href');
        var isExternal = href 
          && !href.startsWith(window.location.origin)
          && !href.startsWith('/');

        if (isExternal) {
          e.preventDefault();
          window.open(href, '_blank');
        }
      });
    }
  });
</script>

<!-- /end HFCM by 99 Robots -->

<!-- Notification Popup -->
<div id="notification-popup" style="display: none;">Updates available. Press to reload</div>

<!-- Horizontal Bar at the Top -->
<div id="top-bar" style="display: none;"></div>

<script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/moment.js/2.29.4/moment.min.js"></script>

<script id="notification">
moment.updateLocale('en', {
  relativeTime: {
    future: "in %s",
    past: "%s ago",
    s: "just now",
    m: "1 min",
    mm: "%d mins",
    h: "1 hr",
    hh: "%d hrs",

<script>
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
  const INTERNAL_JSON_URL = '/wp-json/rss-viewer/v1/latest/';
  const CHECK_INTERVAL = 5 * 60 * 1000;

  let lastKnownArticleID = localStorage.getItem('lastKnownArticleID') || null;
  let newArticleDetected = false;
  let firstLoad = true;
  let isRefreshing = false;

  // ✅ Crash detector (non-blocking)
  window.addEventListener('error', (e) => {
    console.warn('notify script error:', e?.message || e);
  });
  window.addEventListener('unhandledrejection', (e) => {
    console.warn('notify promise rejection:', e?.reason || e);
  });

  // ✅ Hard guard: if rss_ajax is missing, don't let the whole file explode later.
  if (!window.rss_ajax || !rss_ajax.ajax_url) {
    console.warn('rss_ajax.ajax_url missing — notification script disabled');
    return;
  }

  /* ----------------- Chips refresh trigger (delegates to RSS plugin JS) ----------------- */
  function refreshRssChips(reason = '') {
    try {
      // Preferred: call the function exposed by your RSS plugin script
      if (window.gpRss && typeof window.gpRss.refreshChips === 'function') {
        return window.gpRss.refreshChips(reason);
      }
      // Fallback: fire an event the RSS plugin script can listen for
      document.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('grandpx:refreshChips', { detail: { reason } }));
    } catch (e) {}
    return Promise.resolve();
  }

  /* ----------------- Timestamps ----------------- */
  function updateTimestamps() {
    jQuery.ajax({
      url: '/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php?action=get_article_timestamps',
      method: 'GET',
      success: function(response) {
        if (response.success) {
          const timestamps = response.data;
          jQuery('.rss-articles-grid .rss-article-box').each(function() {
            const articleID = jQuery(this).data('post-id');
            if (timestamps[articleID]) {
              const timeAgoElement = jQuery(this).find('.rss-article-lower.publisher-time-wrapper > p');
              const timestamp = timestamps[articleID];
              timeAgoElement.text(moment(timestamp).fromNow());
            }
          });
        } else {
          console.warn('Failed to fetch timestamps');
        }
      },
      error: function(error) {
        console.warn('Error fetching timestamps:', error);
      }
    });
  }

  setInterval(updateTimestamps, 60 * 1000);
  updateTimestamps();

  /* ----------------- New article check ----------------- */
  async function checkForNewArticles() {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(INTERNAL_JSON_URL, { credentials: 'same-origin' });
      const data = await res.json();
      const latestArticleID = data.latest_article_id;

      if (!firstLoad && lastKnownArticleID && latestArticleID !== lastKnownArticleID) {
        const filtered = window.gpNotify && typeof window.gpNotify.isFilteredNow === 'function'
          ? window.gpNotify.isFilteredNow()
          : false;

        if (filtered) {
          if (window.gpNotify && typeof window.gpNotify.queueUpdate === 'function') {
            window.gpNotify.queueUpdate();
          }
          refreshRssChips('new-articles-detected-queued');
        } else {
          newArticleDetected = true;
          showNotification();
          refreshRssChips('new-articles-detected');
        }
      }

      localStorage.setItem('lastKnownArticleID', latestArticleID);
      lastKnownArticleID = latestArticleID;
    } catch (err) {
      console.warn('Error fetching latest article id:', err);
    }
    firstLoad = false;
  }

  // ✅ FIX: robust visibility check + stop queued fades
  function showNotification() {
    const popup  = $('#notification-popup');
    const topBar = $('#top-bar');
    const fade   = 500;

    if (newArticleDetected && !popup.is(':visible')) {
      popup.stop(true,true).fadeIn(fade);
      topBar.stop(true,true).fadeIn(fade);
      $('#grayscale-overlay').stop(true,true).fadeIn(fade);
    }
  }

  /* ------------------------------------------------------------------
     Popup Gatekeeper: never show update popup while a chip/filter is active
  ------------------------------------------------------------------ */
  (function popupGatekeeper() {
    const $popup  = $('#notification-popup');
    const $topBar = $('#top-bar');
    const $overlay = $('#grayscale-overlay');

    if (!$popup.length) return;

    let wasBlockedWhileFiltered = false;
    window.gpNotify = window.gpNotify || {};
    window.gpNotify.queueUpdate = function () { wasBlockedWhileFiltered = true; };
    window.gpNotify.isFilteredNow = isFilteredNow;

    let suppress = false;

    function isFilteredNow() {
      // 1) Best source: plugin API
      try {
        if (window.gpRss && typeof window.gpRss.getFilter === 'function') {
          const f = window.gpRss.getFilter();
          return !!(f && f.type && f.type !== 'all');
        }
      } catch (e) {}

      // 2) DOM fallback: your plugin stores filter state here
      const gridType = $('.rss-articles-grid').attr('data-filter-type');
      if (gridType && gridType !== 'all') return true;

      const barType = $('#rss-chip-bar').attr('data-filter-type');
      if (barType && barType !== 'all') return true;

      return false;
    }

    function forceHide() {
      $popup.stop(true,true).hide();
      $topBar.stop(true,true).hide();
      $overlay.stop(true,true).hide();
    }

    function isVisible() {
      return $popup.is(':visible');
    }

    function check() {
      if (suppress) return;

      const filtered = isFilteredNow();
      const visible  = isVisible();

      // Popup is trying to appear while filtered → kill it
      if (filtered && visible) {
        wasBlockedWhileFiltered = true;
        suppress = true;
        forceHide();
        setTimeout(() => suppress = false, 50);
        return;
      }

      // Filter cleared → release queued popup once
      if (!filtered && wasBlockedWhileFiltered && !visible) {
        wasBlockedWhileFiltered = false;
        newArticleDetected = true;
        showNotification();
      }
    }

    new MutationObserver(check).observe($popup[0], {
      attributes: true,
      attributeFilter: ['style','class']
    });

    window.addEventListener('gp:filterchange', check);
    setInterval(check, 300);
    check();
  })();

  /* ----------------- Helpers (SAFE / optional) ----------------- */

  function reloadDiv(selector, url) {
    const $div = $(selector);
    if (!$div.length) {
      console.log(`⏭️ Skipping reload — ${selector} not found`);
      return $.Deferred().resolve().promise();
    }

    console.log(`Reloading ${selector} from ${url}`);
    return $div.fadeOut(300).promise().then(() => {
      return $div.empty().load(url + ' ' + selector, function(_response, status, xhr) {
        if (status !== 'success') {
          console.warn(`⚠️ Reload status for ${selector}:`, xhr?.status, xhr?.statusText);
        }
        $div.fadeIn(300);
      });
    });
  }

  function refreshCaro() {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      const $caro = $('.caro');
      if (!$caro.length) {
        console.log('⏭️  .caro not present — skipping carousel refresh');
        return resolve();
      }
      console.log('Refreshing .caro component…');
      $caro.fadeOut(300, function() {
        const parent = $(this).parent();
        const originalID = $(this).attr('id');
        $(this).remove();
        parent.append($(`<rssapp-carousel class="caro" style="min-height: 250px; z-index: 2;" id="${originalID}"></rssapp-carousel>`));
        setTimeout(() => {
          if (typeof window.initCarousel === 'function') window.initCarousel();
          resolve();
        }, 500);
      });
    });
  }

  function refreshTicker() {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      const $ticker = $('rssapp-ticker');
      if (!$ticker.length) {
        console.log('⏭️  <rssapp-ticker> not present — skipping');
        return resolve();
      }
      console.log('Refreshing <rssapp-ticker>…');
      $ticker.fadeOut(300, function() {
        const parent = $(this).parent();
        const id = $(this).attr('id');
        $(this).remove();
        parent.append($(`<rssapp-ticker style="max-width: 600px;" id="${id}"></rssapp-ticker>`));
        setTimeout(() => {
          if (typeof window.initTicker === 'function') window.initTicker();
          resolve();
        }, 500);
      });
    });
  }

  function refreshCFFWrapper() {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      const $cff = $('.cff-item');
      if (!$cff.length) {
        console.log('⏭️  .cff-item not present — skipping');
        return resolve();
      }
      console.log('Reloading .cff-wrapper…');
      const original = $cff.html();
      $cff.fadeOut(300, function() {
        $(this).empty().append(original).fadeIn(300, () => {
          if (typeof window.initCFF === 'function') window.initCFF();
          resolve();
        });
      });
    });
  }

  /* ----------------- Core refresh pieces ----------------- */

  function loadArticles(reset = false) {
    if (reset) $('.rss-articles-grid').html('');

    return $.post(rss_ajax.ajax_url, { action: 'load_more_rss_articles', paged: 1 })
      .done(function(response) {
        if (response && response.success) {
          $('.rss-articles-grid').append(response.data.html);
        } else {
          console.warn('Failed to load articles:', response);
        }

        if (window.gpRss && typeof window.gpRss.captureAllCacheFromDom === 'function') {
          requestAnimationFrame(function () {
            try {
              const f = window.gpRss.getFilter ? window.gpRss.getFilter() : null;
              if (!f || f.type === 'all') {
                window.gpRss.captureAllCacheFromDom('notify:loadArticles-after-append');
              }
            } catch (e) {}
          });
        }
      })
      .fail(function(error) {
        console.warn('AJAX error loading articles:', error);
      });
  }

  function loadSummaries(reset = false) {
    if (reset) $('.news-summary-container').html('');
    return $.post(rss_ajax.ajax_url, { action: 'load_more_summaries', paged: 1 })
      .done(function(response) {
        if (response.success) $('.news-summary-container').append(response.data.html);
        else console.warn('Failed to load summaries:', response);
      })
      .fail(function(error) { console.warn('AJAX error loading summaries:', error); });
  }
				  function refreshF1Standings() {
    return fetch(rss_ajax.ajax_url + '?action=get_f1_standings&t=' + Date.now())
      .then(r => r.json())
      .then(result => {
        if (!(result?.success && result?.data)) return;
        document.querySelectorAll('.f1-standings-container').forEach(el => el.removeAttribute('data-initialized'));
        document.dispatchEvent(new Event('fullscreenMenuOpened'));
      })
      .catch(function() {}); // optional
  }

  function refreshDriverMonitor() {
    return $.ajax({
      url: '/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php',
      method: 'POST',
      data: { action: 'refresh_driver_monitor' },
      dataType: 'json'
    }).done(function(response) {
      if (!response?.success || !response?.data?.drivers) return;
      const drivers = response.data.drivers;
      const maxPct  = response.data.max;

      const rowsHtml = drivers.map(d => `
        <div class="f1-monitor-row">
          <div class="f1-monitor-info">
            <span class="f1-monitor-name">${d.abbr}</span>
            <div class="f1-monitor-bar">
              <div class="progress-fill" style="width:0%"></div>
            </div>
            <span class="f1-monitor-percentage" data-target="${d.percentage}">0%</span>
          </div>
          <span class="f1-monitor-sentiment ${String(d.sentiment).toLowerCase()}">${d.sentiment}</span>
        </div>
      `).join("");

      const $rows = $('.f1-monitor-container .f1-monitor-rows');
      $rows.fadeOut(200, function() {
        $rows.html(rowsHtml).fadeIn(300, function() {
          $rows.find('.f1-monitor-row').each(function() {
            const $row = $(this);
            const pct  = parseFloat($row.find('.f1-monitor-percentage').data('target'));
            const scaled = (pct / maxPct) * 100;
            $row.find('.progress-fill').animate({ width: scaled + '%' }, 1000);
            let val = 0, step = pct / 50, $num = $row.find('.f1-monitor-percentage');
            const timer = setInterval(() => {
              val += step;
              if (val >= pct) { val = pct; clearInterval(timer); }
              $num.text(Math.round(val) + '%');
            }, 20);
          });
        });
      });
    }).fail(function() {}); // optional
  }

  function markNewArticles(previouslyLoadedArticles) {
    $('.rss-article-box').each(function() {
      const id = $(this).data('post-id');
      if (!previouslyLoadedArticles.includes(id)) {
        $(this).addClass('new-article').prepend('<span class="new-dot"></span>');
      }
    });
  }

  function removeNewDotOnView() {
    $('.rss-article-box.new-article').each(function() {
      const $box = $(this);
      const rect = $box[0].getBoundingClientRect();
      const winH = $(window).height();
      if (rect.top >= winH * 0.3 && rect.bottom <= winH * 0.7) {
        $box.removeClass('new-article').find('.new-dot').remove();
      }
    });
  }
  $(window).on('scroll', removeNewDotOnView);

  /* ----------------- Master refresh (critical vs optional) ----------------- */

  function refreshContent() {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      $('#loading-bubble').fadeIn();

      const previouslyLoadedArticles = $('.rss-articles-grid .rss-article-box')
        .map(function(){ return $(this).data('post-id'); }).get();

      const critical = [
        loadArticles(true),
        loadSummaries(true),
      ];

      const optional = [
        refreshDriverMonitor(),
        refreshF1Standings(),
        refreshCaro(),
        refreshTicker(),
        refreshCFFWrapper(),
        reloadDiv('.caro', window.location.href),
        reloadDiv('.cff-wrapper', window.location.href),
      ];

      Promise.all(critical)
        .then(() => {
          if (window.gpRss && typeof window.gpRss.refreshChips === 'function') {
            return window.gpRss.refreshChips('notification-refresh');
          }
        })
        .then(() => Promise.allSettled(optional))
        .then(() => {
          markNewArticles(previouslyLoadedArticles);

          if (window.gpRss && typeof window.gpRss.captureAllCacheFromDom === 'function') {
            try {
              const f = window.gpRss.getFilter ? window.gpRss.getFilter() : null;
              if (!f || f.type === 'all') {
                window.gpRss.captureAllCacheFromDom('notify:refreshContent-end');
              }
            } catch (e) {}
          }

          $('#loading-bubble, #notification-popup, #top-bar, #grayscale-overlay').fadeOut();
          newArticleDetected = false;
          isRefreshing = false;
          resolve();
        })
        .catch((err) => {
          console.error('❌ Critical refresh failed:', err);
          $('#loading-bubble, #notification-popup, #top-bar, #grayscale-overlay').fadeOut();
          newArticleDetected = false;
          isRefreshing = false;
          reject(err);
        });
    });
  }

  /* ----------------- Click wiring ----------------- */

  $('#notification-popup').off('click.pluginRefresh').on('click.pluginRefresh', function() {
    if (isRefreshing) return;
    isRefreshing = true;

    $('#notification-popup, #top-bar, #grayscale-overlay').fadeOut();

    refreshRssChips('user-click-refresh');

    refreshContent()
      .then(() => {
        // ✅ make this optional so missing f1_ajax never kills the script
        if (!window.f1_ajax || !f1_ajax.ajax_url) return null;
        return $.post(f1_ajax.ajax_url, { action: 'f1_get_next_race_datetime' });
      })
      .then(res => {
        if (!res) return;

        if (res?.success && res?.data?.race_datetime) {
          const el = document.getElementById('race-countdown');
          if (el) {
            el.setAttribute('data-race-datetime', res.data.race_datetime);
            if (typeof recalcDaysLeft === 'function') recalcDaysLeft();
            if (typeof loadRaceDetails === 'function') loadRaceDetails();
          }
        } else {
          console.warn('Could not refresh next race date:', res?.data);
        }
      })
      .catch(err => {
        console.warn('Non-fatal refresh error:', err);
      })
      .finally(() => {
        $('#notification-popup, #top-bar, #grayscale-overlay').fadeOut();
        newArticleDetected = false;
        isRefreshing = false;
      });
  });

  /* ----------------- Schedulers & visibility ----------------- */
  setInterval(checkForNewArticles, CHECK_INTERVAL);
  setInterval(() => refreshRssChips('hourly-ai-refresh'), 60 * 60 * 1000);

  checkForNewArticles();

  window.addEventListener('focus', function() {
    if (newArticleDetected) showNotification();
  });

  document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', function() {
    if (document.visibilityState === 'visible') checkForNewArticles();
  });
});
</script>

<style>
.new-dot {
  position: absolute;
  top: 5px;
  left: 5px;
  width: 8px;
  height: 8px;
  background-color: green;
  border-radius: 50%;
  z-index: 1;
}
.rss-article-box { position: relative; }
</style>

<!-- HFCM by 99 Robots - Snippet # 7050: Preload Articles -->
<script>
(function () {
  // CONFIG
  const PATH_PREFIX = '/news/';
  const MAX_PREFETCH = 6;        // keep low to avoid host/resource complaints
  const IDLE_DELAY_MS = 1200;    // wait a bit after load
  const PREFETCH_ON_TOUCH = true;
  const PREFETCH_ON_IDLE = true;

  // Respect user/network constraints
  const conn = navigator.connection;
  if (navigator.saveData) return;
  if (conn && (conn.effectiveType === '2g' || conn.effectiveType === 'slow-2g')) return;

  // Only run on homepage (adjust if your homepage is not "/")
  const isHome = (location.pathname === '/' || document.body.classList.contains('home'));
  if (!isHome) return;

  const doneKey = 'fl_prefetch_done_v1';
  if (sessionStorage.getItem(doneKey) === '1') return;

  function isLocalNewsUrl(href) {
    try {
      const u = new URL(href, location.origin);
      return u.origin === location.origin && u.pathname.startsWith(PATH_PREFIX);
    } catch (e) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  // Use <link rel="prefetch"> where supported, and fetch() as a fallback warm-up.
  function prefetchUrl(url) {
    // Avoid duplicates
    if (prefetchUrl.seen.has(url)) return;
    prefetchUrl.seen.add(url);

    // Attempt resource hint
    const l = document.createElement('link');
    l.rel = 'prefetch';
    l.as = 'document';
    l.href = url;
    document.head.appendChild(l);

    // Fallback warm-up: fetch the HTML (warms HTTP cache; may also warm SW cache)
    // Note: ignore errors to avoid noisy logs
    fetch(url, { credentials: 'include', cache: 'force-cache' }).catch(function () {});
  }
  prefetchUrl.seen = new Set();

  function getCandidateLinks() {
    // Restrict to links on the homepage content area if you have a wrapper
    // Otherwise this collects all anchors and filters to /news/
    return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('a[href]'))
      .map(a => a.href)
      .filter(isLocalNewsUrl);
  }

  function runPrefetchBatch() {
    const links = getCandidateLinks();
    // De-dupe while preserving order
    const unique = [];
    const seen = new Set();
    for (const href of links) {
      if (!seen.has(href)) { seen.add(href); unique.push(href); }
      if (unique.length >= MAX_PREFETCH) break;
    }
    unique.forEach(prefetchUrl);
    sessionStorage.setItem(doneKey, '1');
  }

  // Best “perceived speed” on mobile: preload on first touch of a local news link
  if (PREFETCH_ON_TOUCH) {
    document.addEventListener('touchstart', function (e) {
      const a = e.target && e.target.closest ? e.target.closest('a[href]') : null;
      if (!a) return;
      if (!isLocalNewsUrl(a.href)) return;
      prefetchUrl(a.href);
    }, { passive: true, capture: true });

    // Hover intent for desktop
    document.addEventListener('mouseover', function (e) {
      const a = e.target && e.target.closest ? e.target.closest('a[href]') : null;
      if (!a) return;
      if (!isLocalNewsUrl(a.href)) return;
      prefetchUrl(a.href);
    }, { passive: true, capture: true });
  }

  // Optional: small idle batch after load to warm a few likely next pages
  if (PREFETCH_ON_IDLE) {
    window.addEventListener('load', function () {
      setTimeout(runPrefetchBatch, IDLE_DELAY_MS);
    });
  }
})();
</script>
<!-- /end HFCM by 99 Robots -->
